msg:During the May Day holiday, I came to Qiandao Lake for a vacation. After careful selection, I chose voco Qiandao Lake Sunshine Hotel, a new light luxury brand under the InterContinental Hotel Group.
Location: Central Lake District | No. 289, Sunshine Road, Qiandao Lake Town
The hotel occupies a small peninsula. Most of the rooms have balconies facing the outer lake. In the room, you can see the lake view trails and multiple terraces around the island. You can enjoy the central lake area without any obstruction. The mountains and rivers are like a central lake view in a painting. The area is slightly larger and has a balcony. The balcony is surrounded on all sides.
Hotel surroundings:
It must be said that voco's geographical location is very good. The hotel is located on the peninsula to ensure privacy and quiet experience. At the same time, it is very close to the surrounding food, drink and entertainment. There are two Hello electric car direct stores within 500 meters from the hotel entrance. One is the Qiandao Lake flagship store. It is convenient to rent a car and ride. The entrance is about 1 kilometer to the left and right. One side is Tianyu and the other side is Xiushui Square, which is convenient for playing. The best experience of this trip is the hotel service. When checking out, the lobby administration will ask if you need a direct high-speed rail bus. The whole service is very considerate and the overall feeling is very comfortable. name:L‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçj‚Äçu‚Äçn

posted:Posted June 19, 2023
msg:One month in advance, I booked the central lake-view king bed room that was generally praised on the app. I arrived at the hotel at 1:30 that day. The entire hotel has an exclusive peninsula, which occupies a large area and is relatively private. When I checked in at the front desk, I asked the front desk for a room with a higher floor. The front desk reported that only the 4th floor has been cleaned, so I asked for a room on the top floor of the 5th floor. I stored my luggage and went to Tianyu Island to play. After a circle, the front desk called in half an hour to say that the room was cleaned and you can come to get the room card. The service attitude is still very good.
Facilities: Although the app shows that it opened in 2017, both the public areas of the hotel and the various facilities in the rooms are relatively new, and it feels like it opened within 2-3 years. Entering the hotel, the overall fragrance makes people feel more comfortable. The lake view in the lobby bar is invincible, the size of the central lake view double bed room is not bad, and the balcony lake view is also invincible, especially on the top floor. The roof of the balcony is made of glass, which is very comfortable. The facilities are also very new, and the bathtub is also a bonus item. It is very comfortable to take a bath at night.

Hygiene: The overall cleanliness of the room did not find any dirty places, and the public area is relatively clean, but I feel that the hotel has a lot of flying insects. When eating afternoon tea in the lobby bar, the flying insects flew onto the dessert, which greatly affected the appetite. I had dinner the next day When I was there, I saw bugs on a plate in the panel area.

Environment: Needless to say, the environment itself is exclusive to the peninsula. The 270¬∞ lake view, whether it is the public area or the lake view of the room, is the best in the central lake area.

Service: I think the overall service needs to be improved. In addition to the professional front desk business, when I arrived at the hotel entrance, there was only someone to welcome the guests, and no one to help with the luggage. This is the first of all five-star hotels I have stayed in. When I had breakfast the next day, there was garbage on the table The plates are piled up, and there is no waiter to take the initiative to collect them. I only see a few waiters chatting and laughing, which makes people feel bad.
The hotel's catering is also not in line with the five-star status. The hotel's buffet is only open for dining on Friday and Saturday nights every week. The intention must be to save costs and avoid the flow of people. I think we can be a little more flexible about this. In fact, if the hotel‚Äôs buffet is not open, the hotel can only order food from the Chinese restaurant. The price and taste may not be as good as restaurants outside the hotel. In addition, I have already eaten fish heads outside at noon, so I ordered one in the lobby bar before dinner. Afternoon tea, the experience was actually very bad. First, I waited for half an hour for a few pieces of cakes, and then the actual items in the package did not match the content of the package, and the quantity was small, the price/performance ratio was not high, and the taste was not outstanding. The flying insects mentioned above, the overall dining experience is very bad. The next morning's breakfast didn't have much variety. Therefore, the hotel still has a lot of room for improvement in terms of catering, because there are still many people who do not want to leave the hotel and eat in the hotel.
The overall experience of the hotel is still in line with the feeling of vacation. The extra points are the invincible lake view everywhere in the hotel and the decoration style that suits the tastes of young people. However, there is still a lot of room for improvement in the hotel's catering and service.
